center\">IRCTC <span style=\"color: #ff0000\">Registration</span> <span style=\"color: #ff0000\">Sign Up</span> and IRCTC <span style=\"color: #ff0000\">Login</span></h2>\n<p><span style=\"color: #333333\"><strong>IRCTC registration</strong> means creating a new account in IRCTC official website www.irctc.co.in. Having a new account in IRCTC through <span style=\"text-decoration: underline\"><strong>IRCTC registration</strong></span> process reduces the effort which we have been putting to book railway window ticket.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"color: #333333\"><strong>IRCTC New Registration </strong>is required to <span style=\"color: #0000ff\"><span style=\"color: #666699\"><a style=\"color: #666699\" href=\"http://pnrstatusirctc.in/how-to-book-railway-train-ticket-online/\">book the ticket using IRCTC online</a></span>.</span>&nbsp;Without doing “<em><strong>IRCTC registration</strong></em>” or&nbsp;<strong>IRCTC Sign Up</strong>, Railway&nbsp;does not allow to book a ticket, in fact it&nbsp;does not allow any single service like&nbsp;<span style=\"color: #000080\"><a style=\"color: #000080\" title=\"PNR Status – Check IRCTC PNR Status Of Indian Railways\" href=\"http://pnrstatusirctc.in/irctc-pnr-status/\">PNR Status Check</a></span>, Train Enquiry,&nbsp;</span>Train Schedule<span style=\"color: #333333\">,<span style=\"color: #666699\">&nbsp;<a style=\"color: #666699\" href=\"http://pnrstatusirctc.in/irctc-ticket-availability-how-to-check-availability/\">IRCTC Please enter the username here, one which you can easily remember. For example, my name is Ankit so I’d prefer entering username such as ‘<em><strong>ankit2015</strong>‘</em></p>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 30px\"><strong><span style=\"color: #ff6600\">Security Questions</span>: </strong>A security question is a mandatory field and very useful for resetting forgotten password. Sometimes it happens that you forget your password so with this feature you can reset your password by answering the security question.</p>\n<blockquote style=\"padding-left: 30px\">\n<p style=\"padding-left: 30px\"><em>Select the security question and enter the rememberable answer in the text field.</em></p>\n</blockquote>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 30px\"><strong><span style=\"color: #ff6600\">First/Last Name</span>:&nbsp;</strong>Enter your first name and last name in this field. Be careful about this field because this field value can not be changed later.</p>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 30px\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600\"><strong>Marital&nbsp;Status</strong></span>: Select the correct value as applicable to you. This value can be changed later.</p>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 30px\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600\"><strong>DOB</strong></span>: Enter your&nbsp;correct date of birth here.</p>\n<h4>Other Details</h4>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 30px\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600\"><strong>Occupation</strong></span>: Enter your occupation here by selecting the value such as Government, Private, Professional etc.</p>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 30px\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600\"><strong>Aadhar Card</strong></span>: It is not mandatory to enter Aadhar Card number but if you have, then please enter.</p>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 30px\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600\"><strong>Email Id</strong></span>: It is a very important field. You must enter the valid email id here as it is very useful to identify you in the IRCTC system. Also needed for resetting your password in future.</p>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 30px\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600\"><strong>Mobile</strong></span>: Enter valid 10 digits mobile number here. This mobile will be verified through OTP (One Time Password) so re-verify it before submitting the form.</p>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 30px\"><span style=\"color: #ff6600\"><strong>Nationality</strong></span>: Select&nbsp;the value&nbsp;as <strong>India</strong> always.</p>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 30px\"><strong><span style=\"color: #ff6600\">Residential Address</span>, Flat/House Number, Country, PIN number, State, City</strong>: Enter your full residential address and other details. These all values can be changed later.</p>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 30px\"><strong><span style=\"color: #ff6600\">Captcha</span>&nbsp;Image Text:</strong> It is an image containing text which asks the user to enter a correct value before submitting the form.
